Initial Row Type Indicator = Note Detail
Row[2] = "The neck was appropriately prepped and draped after a preoperative C-arm image was done to localize the C4-5, C5-6, C6-7 levels.  Skin was then appropriately prepped and draped and as soon as I got the drapes on while completing the set up for the surgery the monitoring technician informed me that there was a significant drop in his left somatosensory as well as motor evoked potentials.  There was a drop in his systolic blood pressure to 70 without any EKG changes.  This responded very well to fluids and in spite of the blood pressure coming up over 100 for a systolic pressure the changes in the signals were not being seen.  There was no significant change in the latency but clearly an 80% drop in the amplitude of the signals only on the left side and not on the right side.  It was clear that the changes were not coming from just the hemodynamic state, but most likely structural in origin.  The left side tape of the shoulder was taken down and the signals continued to stay diminished.  I therefore decided to awaken the patient and evaluate his neurological status before bringing him back for surgery.  He already has significant deficits in the lower extremity and his left upper extremity is stronger than the right extremity preoperatively.  The signal abnormality seen are significant enough that could cause concerns from a clinical status and therefore full evaluation in an awake state is necessary.  He was asked to be reversed for his anesthesia and taken to recovery in stable condition.  His mother was informed of these findings and she is in agreement to have him reevaluated and then brought back to surgery on another day if he is neurologically intact.  Plan will be to keep maintain his systolic blood pressure at his baseline throughout the process of induction as well as during the surgery."
